4e:["$","p",null,{"className":"mt-3 text-gray-300","children":["The §5 data flow describes ",["$","em",null,{"children":"what"}]," moves between spokes. 51:["$","p",null,{"className":"mt-4 text-gray-300","children":[["$","strong",null,{"className":"text-gray-100","children":"Mode gates only the pause, never the gate."}]," ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"execution_mode"}]," (frozen at ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"init_run"}],") is consulted at exactly ONE point: the ",["$","strong",null,{"className":"text-gray-100","children":"post-PASS human-pause decision"}],". 52:["$","p",null,{"className":"mt-3 text-gray-300","children":[["$","strong",null,{"className":"text-gray-100","children":"Cap exhaustion is a hard stop, never ship-last-attempt."}]," At ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"retry_count == retry_cap"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"gmj_check_cap.py"}]," reports exhaustion and the hub emits a hard-stop report naming the failing artifact + the last gate's reason. 53:["$","p",null,{"className":"mt-3 text-gray-300","children":[["$","strong",null,{"className":"text-gray-100","children":"Run-scoped state relocation."}]," State moves from a single ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":".pipeline/state.json"}]," to a per-run ",["$","strong",null,{"className":"text-gray-100","children":["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"<root>/runs/<run_id>/state.json"}]}]," (",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"<root>"}]," resolved as above — ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":".pipeline"}]," is the illustrative default, not the only path), which holds the resumable run state (",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"current_step"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"completed_steps"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"gate_results"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"offer_spec_path"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"offer_spec_hash"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"retry_counts"}],", plus the Phase-7 frozen keys ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"execution_mode"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"retry_cap"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"run_id"}],") alongside the logged ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"gate_result"}]," audit artifacts (",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"gate_<node>_<type>_<attempt>.json"}],"). ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"run_id"}]," is sanitized to a safe charset before it becomes a directory name (no path traversal), and ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"<root>/runs/<run_id>/"}]," is git-ignored (per-run state + gate logs stay local), where ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"<root>"}]," defaults to ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":".pipeline"}]," but is configurable via ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"pipeline-dir"}],"/",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"GMJ_PIPELINE_DIR"}],"."]}]
54:["$","p",null,{"className":"mt-3 text-gray-300","children":[["$","strong",null,{"className":"text-gray-100","children":"Per-artifact-type state isolation (Phase 32, ARTF-01/04)."}]," A single-offer run produces the full default artifact set (CV, cover letter, interview-prep) by default; each requested type gets its own ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"<root>/runs/<run_id>-{cv,cl,ip}/state.json"}],", derived and validated by ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"scripts/pipeline/gmj_pipeline_run.py"}]," (mirroring ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"gmj_batch.py"}],"'s per-(offer, artifact_type) run_id pattern) — never one shared file, because ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"gate_results"}]," is keyed flatly by DAG node name with no artifact-type dimension (",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"gmj_record_gate.py"}],"), and a shared file would let a later type's gate write clobber an earlier type's recorded verdict. 55:["$","h4",null,{"className":"mt-6 text-lg font-semibold text-gray-100","children":"Parallel fan-out, sequential gates"}]
56:["$","p",null,{"className":"mt-3 text-gray-300","children":["Independent work is dispatched as ",["$","strong",null,{"className":"text-gray-100","children":["parallel ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"Task"}]," calls in a single hub turn"]}]," — ranking ",["$","strong",null,{"className":"text-gray-100","children":"N offers"}],", and composing the ",["$","strong",null,{"className":"text-gray-100","children":"3 artifact types"}]," (CV / cover letter / interview-prep), each with its own output path and its own isolated ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"retry_counts[offer][type]"}]," slot. This is orchestrated task fan-out on Claude Code's single-threaded event loop — not OS threads."]}]

58:["$","h4",null,{"className":"mt-6 text-lg font-semibold text-gray-100","children":"Bounded concurrent-offer dispatch (Phase 35, CONC-01..06)"}]
59:["$","p",null,{"className":"mt-3 text-gray-300","children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"/gmj-batch"}]," extends the same fan-out idiom across ",["$","strong",null,{"className":"text-gray-100","children":"offers"}],", not just artifact types. A batch's ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"max_parallel_offers"}]," (default 3, ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"config/pipeline.config.yaml"}],") is frozen into the batch manifest at ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"gmj_batch.py init"}]," — the same freeze-once pattern as ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"execution_mode"}],"/",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"retry_cap"}],". The deterministic decision of ",["$","em",null,{"children":"which offers may dispatch right now"}]," belongs entirely to ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"scripts/pipeline/gmj_dispatch_cap.py"}]," (never the model): given the manifest, each offer's 3 per-(offer, artifact_type) run states, and the frozen cap, it classifies every offer as TERMINAL / FRESH / ACTIVE and returns the dispatchable run_ids plus free capacity. The hub loop is ",["$","strong",null,{"className":"text-gray-100","children":["ask cap script → dispatch up to that many offers' next steps as parallel ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"Task"}]," calls in one hub turn → mark each terminal completion (",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"gmj_batch.py mark"}],", concurrent-safe ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"batch_manifest.json"}]," writes) → immediately re-ask the cap script (greedy refill)"]}]," — repeated until every offer's 3 runs reach a terminal status. Each offer still runs the unmodified single-offer loop above, per artifact type, with its own isolated ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"retry_counts[offer][type]"}]," slot; Gate A/Gate B remain non-bypassable per-offer-per-type, so concurrency introduces no shared/aggregate gate shortcut. One offer's pipeline failure (gate exhaustion, error) is isolated — it never stalls or corrupts a sibling offer's run in the same wave. Concurrency is implemented purely as multiple ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"Task"}]," calls issued in one hub turn, ",["$","strong",null,{"className":"text-gray-100","children":"never"}]," as a per-offer nested sub-orchestrator, which would violate the hub-and-spoke single-",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"Task"}],"-holder invariant (§2, §6)."]}]

180:["$","h4",null,{"className":"mt-6 text-lg font-semibold text-gray-100","children":"Artifact-only handoff"}]
181:["$","p",null,{"className":"mt-2 text-gray-300","children":["Spokes exchange ",["$","strong",null,{"className":"text-gray-100","children":"typed file-artifact paths, never transcripts or conversation"}],". 182:["$","h4",null,{"className":"mt-6 text-lg font-semibold text-gray-100","children":"Deterministic two-layer control plane"}]
183:["$","p",null,{"className":"mt-2 text-gray-300","children":["A deterministic layer of small, single-purpose Python scripts (exit ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"0"}],"/",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"1"}],", no LLM, no network) makes every safety decision; the LLM layer (",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"gmj-orchestrator"}],") dispatches spokes and calls those scripts via ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"Bash"}],". The model never decides whether a gate passed, whether the retry cap is hit, or whether an artifact is deliverable."]}]
184:["$","h3",null,{"className":"mt-8 text-xl font-bold text-gray-100","children":"Anti-drift principles"}]
185:["$","p",null,{"className":"mt-3 text-gray-300","children":"Beyond the committed floor (isolated context per spoke, typed-file handoff, mandatory gates), three enforceable measures guard against the multi-agent failure modes:"}]
186:["$","ol",null,{"className":"mt-2 list-disc list-inside space-y-1 text-gray-300","children":[" ",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"className":"text-gray-100","children":"Input budget."}]," Each spoke declares a bounded maximum input size. Over-budget input is a contract violation, not a soft warning — it prevents context bloat from silently re-introducing cross-task drift."]}]," ",["$","li",null,{"children":[["$","strong",null,{"className":"text-gray-100","children":"No-progress early-stop."}]," An enhance/retry cycle that makes no measurable gate-metric progress stops early rather than burning the full retry cap. 188:["$","h4",null,{"className":"mt-6 text-lg font-semibold text-gray-100","children":"Dual-mode execution with a retry cap"}]
189:["$","p",null,{"className":"mt-2 text-gray-300","children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"execution_mode"}]," is frozen at run start and gates ",["$","strong",null,{"className":"text-gray-100","children":"only"}]," the post-PASS human pause: ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"human_in_the_loop"}]," pauses for approval after a gate passes; ",["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"autonomous"}]," proceeds automatically. 18a:["$","h4",null,{"className":"mt-6 text-lg font-semibold text-gray-100","children":"Parallel fan-out, sequential gates"}]

18d:["$","p",null,{"className":"mt-2 text-gray-300","children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"text-emerald-400","children":"/gmj-batch"}]," extends the same fan-out idiom across offers, not just artifact types.
